***укрепиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрепиться.html>укрепи́ться</a> (16329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепить.html>укрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепиться.html>укрепи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrepítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепляться.html>укрепля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become stronger, to consolidate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепиться.html>укрепи́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó zdoróvʹje <b>ukrepílosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his health improved [became stronger]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fortify one's position</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепить.html>укрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***укрепление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрепление.html>укрепле́ние</a> (5857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепить.html>укрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепление.html>укрепле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukreplénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепление.html>укрепле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепление.html>укрепле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепление.html>укрепле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strengthening, consolidation, reinforcement</li>
<li>fortification, stockade</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрепляться.html>укрепля́ться</a> (20306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укреплять.html>укрепля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепляться.html>укрепля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrepljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрепиться.html>укрепи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become stronger, to consolidate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fortify one's position</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укреплять.html>укрепля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***укроп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a> (21605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukróp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́пов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укро́пка</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укро́пный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dill (<i>Anethum graveolens</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огородный.html>огоро́дный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukróp</b> ogoródnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/garden_dill" class="extiw" title="w:garden dill">garden dill</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахучий.html>паху́чий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukróp</b> paxúčij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fragrant_dill" class="extiw" title="w:fragrant dill">fragrant dill</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fennel (<i>Foeniculum vulgare</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аптечный.html>апте́чный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukróp</b> aptéčnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pharmacy_dill" class="extiw" title="w:pharmacy dill">pharmacy dill</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b> во́лошский</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukróp</b> vólošskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/voloshsky_dill" class="extiw" title="w:voloshsky dill">voloshsky dill</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukróp</b> sládkij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sweet_fennel" class="extiw" title="w:sweet fennel">sweet fennel</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dropwort (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Oenanthe_aquatica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Oenanthe aquatica"><i>Oenanthe aquatica</i></a></span>, syn <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Oenanthe_phellandrium" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Oenanthe phellandrium"><i>Oenanthe phellandrium</i></a></span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водяной.html>водяно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodjanój <b>ukróp</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/water_fennel" class="extiw" title="w:water fennel">water fennel</a></span></div></dd>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">rock samphire</span> (<i>Crithmum maritimum</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морской.html>морско́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morskój <b>ukróp</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><span class="Latn" lang="en">rock samphire</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mayweed (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Anthemis_cotula" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Anthemis cotula"><i>Anthemis cotula</i></a></span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачий.html>соба́чий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáčij <b>ukróp</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dog_fennel" class="extiw" title="w:dog fennel">dog fennel</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sulphurweed" class="extiw" title="w:sulphurweed">sulphurweed</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Peucedanum_officinale" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Peucedanum officinale"><i>Peucedanum officinale</i></a></span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">каба́ний <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kabánij <b>ukróp</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/hog%27s_fennel" class="extiw" title="w:hog | s fennel">hog’s fennel</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">горични́к <a href = vnd.unilang:аптечный.html>апте́чный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">goričník aptéčnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brimstone-wort" class="extiw" title="w:brimstone-wort">brimstone-wort</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Ukrainian (member of a side of the war in Donbass since 2014)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прочь.html>прочь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> Донбасса, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ruki pročʹ ot Donbassa, <b>ukróp</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't touch Donbass, Ukrainian!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The partitive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́пу</a></i> is used only with the meaning "dill", not "Ukrainian".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***укротить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укротить.html>укроти́ть</a> (23648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крот.html>кро́т</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krót(kij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укротить.html>укроти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrotítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрощать.html>укроща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tame</li>
<li>to subdue, to control, to curb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укротить.html>укроти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инфляция.html>инфля́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukrotítʹ</b> infljáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to curb inflation; bring inflation under control</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***укрощать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрощать.html>укроща́ть</a> (31696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укротить.html>укроти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрощать.html>укроща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukroščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укротить.html>укроти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tame</li>
<li>to subdue, to control, to curb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрощать.html>укроща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инфляция.html>инфля́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukroščátʹ</b> infljáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to curb inflation; bring inflation under control</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укроще́ние</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukroščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укротитель.html>укроти́тель</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukrotítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укроти́мый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukrotímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неукротимый.html>неукроти́мый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neukrotímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрываться.html>укрыва́ться</a> (15949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрывать.html>укрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрываться.html>укрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыться.html>укры́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover/wrap oneself</li>
<li>to seek shelter, to find/take shelter/cover, to take cover</li>
<li>to escape</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрывать.html>укрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***укрытие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тие</a> (7577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыть.html>укры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrýtije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>covering, wrapping</li>
<li>concealment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:источник.html>исто́чников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доход.html>дохо́да</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukrýtije</b> istóčnikov doxóda</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">concealment of one's sources of income</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cover, shelter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огня́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukrýtije</b> ot ognjá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">cover (from fire)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдение.html>наблюде́ния</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukrýtije</b> ot nabljudénija</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">cover/concealment from view</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрытие.html>укры́тии</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ukrýtii</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">under cover</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыть.html>укры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыться.html>укры́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрываться.html>укрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover/wrap oneself</li>
<li>to seek shelter, to find/take shelter/cover, to take cover</li>
<li>to escape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыться.html>укро́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot nevó ništó ne <b>ukrójetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">nothing escapes him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрыть.html>укры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***уксус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксус</a> (13146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">уксусъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uksusŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄξος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óxos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vinegar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úksus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксуса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксусов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vinegar</li></ol>

***укутавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укутавший.html>уку́тавший</a> (14702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укутавший.html>уку́тавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukútavšij</span>)
